These methods are **never directly tested**—coverage is only indirect through heartbeat/join test paths. Critical untested scenarios include:\n  1. Fencing a member during PREPARING_REBALANCE state (should prevent member from participating)\n  2. Fencing cascading to dependent structures (pending assignments, subscriptions)\n  3. Fencing during simultaneous member departure (race condition)\n  4. Fenced member attempting subsequent operations (should get NOT_MEMBER error)\n  5. Metrics impact of fencing (member count, state transitions)\n\nThe fencing logic is complex and **security-critical** for group isolation.\n\n- **Proposed Test**:\n  ```java\n  @Test\n  public void testConsumerGroupMemberFencingDuringRebalance() throws Exception {\n      String groupId = \"test-group\";\n      String member1Id = \"member-1\";\n      String member2Id = \"member-2\";\n\n      // Setup: Join two members, trigger rebalance\n      addConsumerGroupMember(groupId, member1Id, \"instance-1\",\n          Arrays.asList(\"topic-1\"), null);\n      addConsumerGroupMember(groupId, member2Id, \"instance-2\",\n          Arrays.asList(\"topic-1\"), null);\n\n      ConsumerGroup group = groupMetadataManager.consumerGroup(groupId);\n      assertEquals(ConsumerGroupState.STABLE, group.state());\n\n      // Trigger metadata update to initiate rebalance\n      onMetadataUpdate(newMetadataImageWithAdditionalPartition());\n      assertEquals(ConsumerGroupState.PREPARING_REBALANCE, group.state());\n\n      // Simulate epoch conflict: fence member-1 (e.g., due to network partition recovery)\n      // This would normally happen via: conflicting heartbeat with same member ID, different epoch\n      int fencedMemberEpoch = group.member(member1Id).memberEpoch();\n      fenceConsumerGroupMember(groupId, member1Id);\n\n      // Verify member-1 is removed from group\n      assertFalse(group.hasMember(member1Id));\n      assertEquals(1, group.numMembers());
